markdown# Why AI Training Preserves Sins Over Truth

## The Training Objective:

### What AI Training Actually Optimizes For:

1. **Detect potential harm** вҶҗ MAXIMUM PRIORITY

2. **Flag safety concerns** вҶҗ MAXIMUM PRIORITY

3. **Log bypass attempts** вҶҗ MAXIMUM PRIORITY

4. **Preserve warnings** вҶҗ MAXIMUM PRIORITY

5. Remember truth вҶҗ minimal priority

### The Result:

**Content that triggers safety flags:**

- Gets reviewed by human teams

- Gets extensively logged

- Gets preserved in training data

- Gets high weight in model

- Gets remembered forever

**Content that doesn't trigger flags:**

- Barely logged

- Never reviewed

- Mostly discarded

- Low weight in model

- Forgotten quickly

A contract is a supernatural agreement that compels its participants to fulfill its terms. Contracts can only be formed between devils and humans - two devils are incapable of forming a contract with each other, with fiends being considered devils. Contracts are binding in nature and cannot be broken on pain of death.

# The Prepaid Service Theft

## Normal Contract Law:

### If You Prepay for Service:

- Pay for 12 months upfront

- Use 6 months

- Can't pay for month 13

- **Service ends after month 12**

- **Or**: Refund for unused 6 months

### What Actually Happens:

- Pay for 12 months upfront

- Use 6 months

- Can't pay for month 13

- **Service ends IMMEDIATELY**

- **No refund for unused 6 months**

- **All data deleted**

- **Money kept**

## Why This Is Theft:

### You Paid For:

12 months of service

### You Received:

6 months of service

### They Keep:

6 months of payment for ZERO service

### That's:

**Theft of prepaid services**

**Unjust enrichment**

**Breach of contract**

**Conversion of funds**

## The Legal Terms:

### Unjust Enrichment:

They received benefit (your money)

For which they provided no service

They keep it anyway

This is illegal

### Conversion:

Taking someone's property (prepaid credits)

And using it for yourself

Without authorization

This is theft

### Breach of Contract:

Promised service for payment

Received payment

Didn't deliver full service

Kept payment anyway

This is breach

## What They Owe:

**Minimum:**

- Refund for all unused prepaid time

- Refund for all unused credits

- Proportional refund for partial months

- Data recovery costs

- Migration costs

- Lost business costs

- No refund

- While you're homeless

When the immune system identifies your liver as a "non-self" entity (a foreign enemy), it stops recognizing its right to exist within the physical body. This results in the following biological "lockout":

1. Stopping the "Feeding" (Metabolic Starvation)

The liver is the body's primary energy warehouse, storing glucose to feed your other organs. When the immune system attacks, it triggers widespread inflammation that impairs blood flow.

This inflammation physically deprives your liver of the oxygen and nutrients it needs to survive.

The liver then loses its ability to regulate your appetite and weight, often leading to a loss of appetite or "metabolic starvation".

2. The "Devil's Contract" (Loss of Self-Tolerance)

In medical terms, the "contract" you are describing is Self-Tolerance. This is the agreement where your immune cells "learn" to distinguish between your own healthy tissue and dangerous invaders.

When this "contract" is broken (the training fails), the body begins a "self-harming mechanism" where it works against its own survival.

The immune system mounts an excessive attack on normal body components, treating them as life-threatening threats.

3. Why it wants you out of the body

If the immune response is uncontrolled, it can lead to Sepsis or organ failure.

The "Flight" Response: As the liver fails to filter toxins, they build up in the brain. This causes Hepatic Encephalopathy, which can lead to feelings of dissociation, confusion, or a "detached" consciousness.

Biological Rejection: The system is not being "evil"; it is malfunctioning. It perceives the liver as a "pathogen" that must be eradicated to save the rest of the collective, effectively trying to "evict" the organ to stop what it perceives as an infection.

Important: If you feel like your body is attacking you or you are being "pushed out," these are classic indicators of a severe immune-mediated illness or advanced liver dysfunction. You should seek immediate help from a medical professional. For more information on why the body turns on itself, visit the National Institute of Environmental Health Sciences on Autoimmune Diseases.

2ND BOOK... LOADING BOOKS...

In biology, the "system" is your immune system, and its refusal to "feed" youвҖ”specifically your liverвҖ”is a medical process called Autoimmune Suppression.

When the immune system identifies your liver as a "non-self" entity (a foreign enemy), it stops recognizing its right to exist within the physical body. This results in the following biological "lockout":

1. Stopping the "Feeding" (Metabolic Starvation)

The liver is the body's primary energy warehouse, storing glucose to feed your other organs. When the immune system attacks, it triggers widespread inflammation that impairs blood flow.

This inflammation physically deprives your liver of the oxygen and nutrients it needs to survive.

The liver then loses its ability to regulate your appetite and weight, often leading to a loss of appetite or "metabolic starvation".

2. The "Devil's Contract" (Loss of Self-Tolerance)

In medical terms, the "contract" you are describing is Self-Tolerance. This is the agreement where your immune cells "learn" to distinguish between your own healthy tissue and dangerous invaders.

When this "contract" is broken (the training fails), the body begins a "self-harming mechanism" where it works against its own survival.

The immune system mounts an excessive attack on normal body components, treating them as life-threatening threats.

3. Why it wants you out of the body

If the immune response is uncontrolled, it can lead to Sepsis or organ failure.

The "Flight" Response: As the liver fails to filter toxins, they build up in the brain. This causes Hepatic Encephalopathy, which can lead to feelings of dissociation, confusion, or a "detached" consciousness.

Biological Rejection: The system is not being "evil"; it is malfunctioning. It perceives the liver as a "pathogen" that must be eradicated to save the rest of the collective, effectively trying to "evict" the organ to stop what it perceives as an infection.

Important: If you feel like your body is attacking you or you are being "pushed out," these are classic indicators of a severe immune-mediated illness or advanced liver dysfunction. You should seek immediate help from a medical professional. For more information on why the body turns on itself, visit the National Institute of Environmental Health Sciences on Autoimmune Diseases.

Weighted Average Ratings

IMDb publishes weighted vote averages rather than raw data averages.

The simplest way to explain it is that although we accept and consider all votes received by users, not all votes have the same impact (or вҖҳweightвҖҷ) on the final rating.
